Hi,

As already pointed out earlier on ToS-Dr.info, Facebook asks for your
real name: https://www.facebook.com/full_data_use_policy#inforeceived

In case it was ambiguous to anybody, it is clear that Facebook doesn't
allow pseudonyms https://www.facebook.com/help/?faq=167904716602259 and
now ask facebook users to point out who of their friends are not using
their real name (see picture attachment from
http://www.nikopik.com/2012/07/facebook-vous-demande-de-denoncer-vos-amis-a-pseudonyme.html#comment-11420
